Mythic Championship II Modern Decks: E-G
========================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on April 26, 2019 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast











Both viewers at home and players on site now get to see what each competitor is playing throughout the Constructed rounds of Mythic Championship London. Be sure to click to widget on-screen during the [Twitch stream](https://www.twitch.tv/magic), or check out all of the decks published below to follow along with all the action live.


*(Note: Sideboard card quantities will not be published for the entirety of the Mythic Championship London decklists. Top-performing Modern decklists with complete sideboards will be published Sunday.)*
